    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">

        $(function (){

        $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();

        var connectstringOut = new Array();

        $('.cb').each(function () {
            const name = $(this).attr("name");
            if (location.search.includes($(this).val())) {
                $(this).prop("checked", true);
                //否則子filter會disabled
                if (name == "cballPrimary")
                    $("input[name='choose_Primary']").prop("disabled", false);
                if (name == "cballMH")
                    $("input[name='choose_MH']").prop("disabled", false);
                if (name == "cballJunior")
                    $("input[name='choose_Junior']").prop("disabled", false);
            }
            if ($(this).prop('checked') === true) {
                connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
            }
        });

        //點擊觸發全選或是全不選
        //有三個選項的全選：低年級、中高年級、國中以上
        $('.cb').click(function () {
            const name = $(this).attr("name");
            if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
                if (name == "cballPrimary") {
                    $("input[name='choose_Primary']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", true);
                        $(this).prop("disabled", false);
                        connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
                    });
                }
                if (name == "cballMH") {
                    $("input[name='choose_MH']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", true);
                        $(this).prop("disabled", false);
                        connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
                    });
                }
                if (name == "cballJunior") {
                    $("input[name='choose_Junior']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", true);
                        $(this).prop("disabled", false);
                        connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
                    });
                }
            }
            else {
                index = connectstringOut.indexOf($(this).val());
                if (index >= 0) {
                    connectstringOut.splice(index, 1);
                }
                if (name === "cballPrimary")
                    $("input[name='choose_Primary']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", false);
                        //$(this).prop("disabled", true);
                        index = connectstringOut.indexOf($(this).val());
                        if (index >= 0) {
                            connectstringOut.splice(index, 1);
                        }
                    });
                if (name === "cballMH")
                    $("input[name='choose_MH']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", false);
                        //$(this).prop("disabled", true);
                        index = connectstringOut.indexOf($(this).val());
                        if (index >= 0) {
                            connectstringOut.splice(index, 1);
                        }
                    });
                if (name === "cballJunior")
                    $("input[name='choose_Junior']").each(function () {
                        $(this).prop("checked", false);
                        //$(this).prop("disabled", true);
                        index = connectstringOut.indexOf($(this).val());
                        if (index >= 0) {
                            connectstringOut.splice(index, 1);
                        }
                    });
            }
        });

        $("#btnSelectAllArea").click(function () {
            if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                $('.cb').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).val() !== "withAudio" &&
                        $(this).val() !== "withGraph" &&
                        $(this).val() !== "withVideo") {
                        $(this).prop("checked", "checked");
                    }
                });
                $("input[name='choose_Primary']").prop("disabled", false);
                $("input[name='choose_MH']").prop("disabled", false);
                $("input[name='choose_Junior']").prop("disabled", false);
            } else {
                $('.cb').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).val() !== "withAudio" &&
                        $(this).val() !== "withGraph" &&
                        $(this).val() !== "withVideo") {
                        $(this).prop("checked", null);
                    }
                });
                $("input[name='choose_Primary']").prop("disabled", "disabled");
                $("input[name='choose_MH']").prop("disabled", "disabled");
                $("input[name='choose_Junior']").prop("disabled", "disabled");
            }
        });

        $("#btnSelectAllMedia").click(function () {
            if ($(this).prop("checked")) {
                $('.cb').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).val() === "withAudio" ||
                        $(this).val() === "withGraph" ||
                        $(this).val() === "withVideo") {
                        $(this).prop("checked", "checked");
                    }
                });
            } else {
                $('.cb').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).val() === "withAudio" ||
                        $(this).val() === "withGraph" ||
                        $(this).val() === "withVideo") {
                        $(this).prop("checked", null);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        let isSelectAllArea = true;
        let isSelectAllMedia = true;

        $('.cb').each(function () {
            if ($(this).val() !== "withAudio" &&
                $(this).val() !== "withGraph" &&
                $(this).val() !== "withVideo" &&
                !$(this).prop("checked")) {
                isSelectAllArea = false;
            }

            if (($(this).val() === "withAudio" ||
                $(this).val() === "withGraph" ||
                $(this).val() === "withVideo") &&
                !$(this).prop("checked")) {
                isSelectAllMedia = false;
            }
        });

        if (isSelectAllArea) {
            $("#btnSelectAllArea").prop("checked", "checked");
        }

        if (isSelectAllMedia) {
            $("#btnSelectAllMedia").prop("checked", "checked");
        }

        if (location.href.includes("order=query")) {
            $('#order_search').css("color", "#c80106");
            $('#order_relate').css("color", "black");
            $('#order_title').css("color", "black");
        }
        else if (location.href.includes("order=keyword_title")) {
            $('#order_title').css("color", "#c80106");
            $('#order_search').css("color", "black");
            $('#order_relate').css("color", "black");
        } else {
            $('#order_title').css("color", "black");
            $('#order_search').css("color", "black");
            $('#order_relate').css("color", "#c80106");
        }

        $('#filter_btn').click(function () {
            var strUrl = "/Home/List/1";

            var order = "keyword_title";
            var orgSearch = "";

            if (location.search.split("order=").length > 1) {
                order = location.search.split("order=")[1].split("&orgSearch=")[0];
                orgSearch = location.search.split("order=")[1].split("&orgSearch=")[1];
            }

            connectstringOut = new Array();

            $('.cb').each(function () {
                if ($(this).prop('checked')) {
                    connectstringOut.push($(this).val());
                }
            });

            if (order === "query"){
                strUrl = strUrl + location.search.split("&")[0] + "&source=" + connectstringOut.join() + "&order=query";
            }
            else if (order === "keyword_title") {
                if (orgSearch && orgSearch.length > 0) {
                    strUrl = "/Home/Search?submitButton=pronounciation&search=" + orgSearch + "&source=" + connectstringOut.join() + "&order=keyword_title&orgSearch=" + orgSearch;
                } else {
                    strUrl = strUrl + location.search.split("&")[0] + "&source=" + connectstringOut.join() + "&order=keyword_title";
                }
            }
            else{
                strUrl = strUrl + location.search.split("&")[0] + "&source=" + connectstringOut.join() + "&order=relevance";
            }

            $.ajax({
                url: "/api/UserBehaviorApi/Index?content=" + encodeURI(connectstringOut.join()) +"&behavior=B026&URL="+encodeURIComponent(strUrl),
                type: "Get",
                success: function (msg) {
                },
                error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                }
            });

            window.location = strUrl;
        });

        $("#order_relate").click(function () {
            const locationurl = location.href.replace("&"+location.search.split("&")[location.search.split("&").length - 1], "").split("&order=")[0] + "&order=relevance";
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/api/UserBehaviorApi/Index?behavior=B027&URL="+encodeURIComponent(locationurl),
                    type: "Get",
                    success: function (msg) {
                    },

        $("#order_search").click(function () {

        const lstIntWordTitleId = [34575,128058,1503,1543,129573,15012,28298,6384,54890,50781,2778,42718,42703,1541,158888,14909,6292,2914,17257,51688,32060,34782,26254,676,22398,7304,24963,1027,13477,21809,42618,1939,17572,48648,46281,27783,8363,715,50401,1468,10225,12455,42066,42705,34581,42741,137635,42702,86726,24367,18696,140229,1668,1542,1688,9417,6158,34457,5714,46044,51286,58342,22432,6928,52414,40475,2839,40041,23656,28307,47345,40196,56940,17297,21096,26830,25886,50167,22004,12960,30770,53390,42487,21502,23747,27838,890,53188,53838,26323,56073,52917,52190,35392,7947,33505,18111,4364,39541,26744];

        for (let intIndex in lstIntWordTitleId)
        {
            $.ajax({
                url: "/api/WordTitleReviewCountApi/?intWordTitleId="+lstIntWordTitleId[intIndex],
                type: "Get",
                success: function (msg) {
                    const strSpanId = "#spanWordViewCount_"+this.url.substring(this.url.lastIndexOf("=") + 1, this.url.length);
                    $(strSpanId).html(msg);
                },
                error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                }
            });

            $.ajax({
                url: "/api/WordBookmarkCountApi/?intWordTitleId="+lstIntWordTitleId[intIndex],
                type: "Get",
                success: function (msg) {
                    const strSpanId = "#spanWordSaveCount_"+this.url.substring(this.url.lastIndexOf("=") + 1, this.url.length);
                    $(strSpanId).html(msg);
                },
                error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                }
            });

    var i = 0;
    $(document).ready(function () {
        const width = $(window).width();

        if (width < 768) {
            $("#advanced").slideUp(500);
            $("#extend").attr("class", "glyphicon glyphicon-circle-arrow-down");
        }
        else {
            $("#advanced").slideDown(500);
            $("#extend").attr("class", "glyphicon glyphicon-circle-arrow-up");
        }
    });

    $(window).resize(function () {
        const width = $(window).width();

        if (width < 1000) {
            $("#n-head1").css("display", "none");
            $("#m-head1").css("display", "inline");
            $("#n-head2").css("display", "none");
            $("#m-head2").css("display", "inline");
        }
        else {
            $("#m-head1").css("display", "none");
            $("#n-head1").css("display", "inline");
            $("#m-head2").css("display", "none");
            $("#n-head2").css("display", "inline");
        }
    });

    $("#extend").click(function () {
        i = i + 1;
        if (i % 2 === 1) {
            $("#advanced").slideUp(500);
            $("#extend").attr("class", "glyphicon glyphicon-circle-arrow-down");
        }
        else {
            $("#advanced").slideDown(500);
            $("#extend").attr("class", "glyphicon glyphicon-circle-arrow-up");
        }
    });
